class TextDetector(object):
    def __init__(self, args):
        self.args = args
        self.det_algorithm = args.det_algorithm
        self.use_onnx = args.use_onnx
        pre_process_list = [{
            'DetResizeForTest': {
                'limit_side_len': args.det_limit_side_len,
                'limit_type': args.det_limit_type,
            }
        }, {
            'NormalizeImage': {
                'std': [0.229, 0.224, 0.225],
                'mean': [0.485, 0.456, 0.406],
                'scale': '1./255.',
                'order': 'hwc'
            }
        }, {
            'ToCHWImage': None
        }, {
            'KeepKeys': {
                'keep_keys': ['image', 'shape']
            }
        }]
        postprocess_params = {}
        if self.det_algorithm == "DB":
            postprocess_params['name'] = 'DBPostProcess'
            postprocess_params["thresh"] = args.det_db_thresh
            postprocess_params["box_thresh"] = args.det_db_box_thresh
            postprocess_params["max_candidates"] = 1000
            postprocess_params["unclip_ratio"] = args.det_db_unclip_ratio
            postprocess_params["use_dilation"] = args.use_dilation
            postprocess_params["score_mode"] = args.det_db_score_mode
            postprocess_params["box_type"] = args.det_box_type
        elif self.det_algorithm == "DB++":
            postprocess_params['name'] = 'DBPostProcess'
            postprocess_params["thresh"] = args.det_db_thresh
            postprocess_params["box_thresh"] = args.det_db_box_thresh
            postprocess_params["max_candidates"] = 1000
            postprocess_params["unclip_ratio"] = args.det_db_unclip_ratio
            postprocess_params["use_dilation"] = args.use_dilation
            postprocess_params["score_mode"] = args.det_db_score_mode
            postprocess_params["box_type"] = args.det_box_type
            pre_process_list[1] = {
                'NormalizeImage': {
                    'std': [1.0, 1.0, 1.0],
                    'mean':
                        [0.48109378172549, 0.45752457890196, 0.40787054090196],
                    'scale': '1./255.',
                    'order': 'hwc'
                }
            }
        elif self.det_algorithm == "EAST":
            postprocess_params['name'] = 'EASTPostProcess'
            postprocess_params["score_thresh"] = args.det_east_score_thresh
            postprocess_params["cover_thresh"] = args.det_east_cover_thresh
            postprocess_params["nms_thresh"] = args.det_east_nms_thresh
        elif self.det_algorithm == "SAST":
            pre_process_list[0] = {
                'DetResizeForTest': {
                    'resize_long': args.det_limit_side_len
                }
            }
            postprocess_params['name'] = 'SASTPostProcess'
            postprocess_params["score_thresh"] = args.det_sast_score_thresh
            postprocess_params["nms_thresh"] = args.det_sast_nms_thresh

            if args.det_box_type == 'poly':
                postprocess_params["sample_pts_num"] = 6
                postprocess_params["expand_scale"] = 1.2
                postprocess_params["shrink_ratio_of_width"] = 0.2
            else:
                postprocess_params["sample_pts_num"] = 2
                postprocess_params["expand_scale"] = 1.0
                postprocess_params["shrink_ratio_of_width"] = 0.3

        elif self.det_algorithm == "PSE":
            postprocess_params['name'] = 'PSEPostProcess'
            postprocess_params["thresh"] = args.det_pse_thresh
            postprocess_params["box_thresh"] = args.det_pse_box_thresh
            postprocess_params["min_area"] = args.det_pse_min_area
            postprocess_params["box_type"] = args.det_box_type
            postprocess_params["scale"] = args.det_pse_scale
        elif self.det_algorithm == "FCE":
            pre_process_list[0] = {
                'DetResizeForTest': {
                    'rescale_img': [1080, 736]
                }
            }
            postprocess_params['name'] = 'FCEPostProcess'
            postprocess_params["scales"] = args.scales
            postprocess_params["alpha"] = args.alpha
            postprocess_params["beta"] = args.beta
            postprocess_params["fourier_degree"] = args.fourier_degree
            postprocess_params["box_type"] = args.det_box_type
        elif self.det_algorithm == "CT":
            pre_process_list[0] = {'ScaleAlignedShort': {'short_size': 640}}
            postprocess_params['name'] = 'CTPostProcess'
        else:
            logger.info("unknown det_algorithm:{}".format(self.det_algorithm))
            sys.exit(0)

        self.preprocess_op = create_operators(pre_process_list)
        self.postprocess_op = build_post_process(postprocess_params)
        self.predictor = utility.TritonInference("PP_OCRv4_det", ['sigmoid_0.tmp_0'])

// ==UserScript==
// @name         小红书-自动点赞脚本2.0.0
// @auther       叶花弈
// @version      2.0.0
// @description  1.小红书内容自动点赞; 2.自动切换到最新分类; 3.已点过的忽略,避免取消点赞; 4.每隔半小时自动刷新。
// @match        https://www.xiaohongshu.com/search_result*
// ==/UserScript==

(function () {
  // ------------------基础入参定义----------------
  let openKeyWord = false; // 是否已经打开UI
  let runStatus = false; // 当前运行状态
  let SLEEP_TIME = 4000; // 点赞间隔
  let SEARCH_END_TIME = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 关键词全部检索完毕后准备重新开始的等待时间
  const sleep = async (t) => new Promise((R) => setTimeout(R, t)); // 异步转同步阻塞函数(延迟Time)
  let alreadyTotal = 0; // 本次脚本运行已经点赞的总数量
  // 模拟搜索行为
  const handleSearch = (keyWord) => {
    console.log(`正在模拟搜索行为......${keyWord}`);
    // 搜索框DOM - 输入
    document.getElementById("search-input").value = keyWord;
    const event = new Event("input", { bubbles: true });
    document.getElementById("search-input").dispatchEvent(event);
    // 搜索按钮DOM - 点击
    document.querySelectorAll(".search-icon")[0].click();
  };
  // 1.生成动态关键词输入UI-------------------------
  // (1.1). 容器
  const keyWordDom = document.createElement("div");
  const keyWordDomStyle = `
          width: 0; height: 0; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden;
          background-color: #f0c9cf; border-radius: 10px;
          position: fixed; right: 50vw; top: 50vh;
          box-shadow: 2px 6px 10px 0px #0e121629;
          transform: translate(50%, -50%); transition: all 0.3s;
      `;
  keyWordDom.style = keyWordDomStyle;
  // (1.2). 标题
  const keyWordTitleDom = document.createElement("div");
  keyWordTitleDom.style = `
          font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; padding: 10px;
        `;
  keyWordTitleDom.innerText = "小红书脚本检索关键词自定义(分号隔开;)";
  // (1.3). 输入文本域
  const keyWordInputArea = document.createElement("textarea");
  keyWordInputArea.style = `
          width: 580px; height: 300px; margin: 8px;
          resize:none; border: none;
        `;
  // (1.4). 状态申明
  const statusDom = document.createElement("div");
  statusDom.innerHTML = "<span style='color: #F56C6C'>当前运行状态: 已暂停(X)</span>";
  statusDom.style = `
          font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; padding-left: 10px;
        `;
  // (1.5). 启动按钮
  const keyWordStartBtn = document.createElement("div");
  keyWordStartBtn.style = `
          width: 60px; font-size: 16px; background-color: rgb(64,158,255);
          border-radius: 6px; padding: 4px; float: right; margin-right: 10px;
          cursor: pointer; text-align: center; color: white;
        `;
  keyWordStartBtn.innerText = "启动";
  keyWordStartBtn.onclick = async () => {
    if (document.querySelectorAll(".login-btn").length > 0) return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 请先登录");
    if (runStatus) return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 请先暂停脚本执行后,再进行启动操作");

    // 1.获取输入文本域内容
    const inputText = keyWordInputArea.value;
    const keyWordAry = inputText.split(";");
    let keyWordIndex = 0;
    if (keyWordAry[keyWordIndex] === "") return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 关键词不能存在空值");
    console.log(`%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]脚本已启动 => 关键词列表: `, "color: green", keyWordAry);
    runStatus = true;
    statusDom.innerHTML = "<span style='color: green'>当前运行状态: 执行中(√)</span>";
    handleSearch(keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]);
    await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
    // 2.将分类切换到最新
    const classDomList = document.querySelectorAll(".dropdown-items .text");
    for (let i = 0; i < classDomList.length; i++) {
      const dom = classDomList[i];
      const { textContent } = dom;
      if (textContent.includes("最新")) {
        dom.click();
        await sleep(3000); // 保证小红书接口请求最新数据后, 再执行后续逻辑
        break;
      }
    }
    // 3.进行点赞
    while (true) {
      // 如果状态为暂停, 则停止点赞行为
      if (!runStatus) break;
      // (3.1).获取点赞爱心DOM
      const likeDomList = document.querySelectorAll(".like-wrapper");
      // (3.2).如果点赞爱心DOM为0, 则相当于(3.5)
      if (likeDomList.length === 0) {
        console.warn("error: 未找到任何点赞按钮-页面DOM缺失,类名[.like-wrapper]");
        keyWordIndex++;
        if (keyWordIndex >= keyWordAry.length) {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]全部关键词已检索完毕,重新开始检索=>下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
          keyWordIndex = 0;
          await sleep(SEARCH_END_TIME);
        } else {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]当前关键词=>${
              keyWordAry[keyWordIndex - 1]
            }<=检索完毕, 切换到下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
        }
        handleSearch(keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]);
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
        continue;
      }
      // (3.3).将点赞爱心DOM排除掉已为点赞状态的DOM, 避免误操作取消点赞
      const waitLikeDomList = Array.from(likeDomList).filter((dom) => {
        const { baseVal } = dom.querySelectorAll("use")[0].href;
        return baseVal === "#like";
      });
      // (3.4).通知即将点赞数量, 执行点赞逻辑,以及通知本页已点赞数量
      console.log("本轮待点赞:", waitLikeDomList.length, "条数据");
      for (let i = 0; i < waitLikeDomList.length; i++) {
        const dom = waitLikeDomList[i];
        dom.click();
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
      }
      alreadyTotal += likeDomList.length;
      // (3.5).如果发现THE_END文案, 说明该分类的检索关键词数据已经全部获取完毕, 进行下一个关键字的检索
      if (document.querySelectorAll(".end-container").length > 0) {
        keyWordIndex++;
        if (keyWordIndex >= keyWordAry.length) {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]全部关键词已检索完毕,重新开始检索=>下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
          keyWordIndex = 0;
          await sleep(SEARCH_END_TIME);
        } else {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]当前关键词=>${
              keyWordAry[keyWordIndex - 1]
            }<=检索完毕, 切换到下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
        }
        handleSearch(keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]);
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
      }
      // (3.6).进行下一页的数据获取
      else {
        // 加载更多待点赞数据
        window.scrollBy(0, window.innerHeight);
        console.log(
          `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]已点赞数量: ${alreadyTotal}, 正在拉取下一页数据`,
          "color: tomato"
        );
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
      }
    }
  };
  // (1.6). 停止按钮
  const keyWordStopBtn = document.createElement("div");
  keyWordStopBtn.style = `
          width: 60px; font-size: 16px; background-color: rgb(245,108,108);
          border-radius: 6px; padding: 4px; float: right; margin-right: 10px;
          cursor: pointer; text-align: center; color: white;
        `;
  keyWordStopBtn.innerText = "暂停";
  keyWordStopBtn.onclick = () => {
    if (!runStatus) return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 当前已暂停运行");
    runStatus = false;
    statusDom.innerHTML = "<span style='color: #F56C6C'>当前运行状态: 已暂停(X)</span>";
  };

  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordTitleDom);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordInputArea);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordStartBtn);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordStopBtn);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(statusDom);
  // 2.生成入口UI-----------------------------------
  const entranceDom = document.createElement("div");
  const baseStyle = `
          position: fixed; right: 0; top: 40vh; cursor: pointer;
          width: 76px; background-color: rgb(212,25,27); white-space: nowrap;
          overflow: hidden; opacity: 0.4; transition: all 0.5s;
          padding: 4px 0px 4px 10px; border-radius: 10px 0px 0px 10px;
          font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; color: white;
          box-shadow: 2px 6px 10px 0px #0e121629;
        `;
  entranceDom.style = baseStyle;
  entranceDom.title = "小红书自动点赞刷新脚本";
  entranceDom.innerText = "小红书 V2.0.0";
  entranceDom.onmouseover = () => {
    entranceDom.style = baseStyle + `opacity: 1; width: 160px;`;
  };
  entranceDom.onmouseleave = () => {
    entranceDom.style = baseStyle;
  };
  entranceDom.onclick = () => {
    openKeyWord = !openKeyWord;
    if (openKeyWord) {
      keyWordDom.style = keyWordDomStyle + "width: 600px; height: 410px; opacity: 0.8;";
    } else {
      keyWordDom.style = keyWordDomStyle + "width: 0; height: 0; opacity: 0;";
    }
  };
  // End: ========注入页面之中========
  document.body.appendChild(entranceDom);
  document.body.appendChild(keyWordDom);
})();

2024-07-17 12:23:25.259 信息:参_信息:群（44765526058@chatroom）wxid_5sakecjc26an21：@小猪 
// ==UserScript==
// @name         小红书-自动点赞脚本2.0.0
// @auther       叶花弈
// @version      2.0.0
// @description  1.小红书内容自动点赞; 2.自动切换到最新分类; 3.已点过的忽略,避免取消点赞; 4.每隔半小时自动刷新。
// @match        https://www.xiaohongshu.com/search_result*
// ==/UserScript==

(function () {
  // ------------------基础入参定义----------------
  let openKeyWord = false; // 是否已经打开UI
  let runStatus = false; // 当前运行状态
  let SLEEP_TIME = 4000; // 点赞间隔
  let SEARCH_END_TIME = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 关键词全部检索完毕后准备重新开始的等待时间
  const sleep = async (t) => new Promise((R) => setTimeout(R, t)); // 异步转同步阻塞函数(延迟Time)
  let alreadyTotal = 0; // 本次脚本运行已经点赞的总数量
  // 模拟搜索行为
  const handleSearch = (keyWord) => {
    console.log(`正在模拟搜索行为......${keyWord}`);
    // 搜索框DOM - 输入
    document.getElementById("search-input").value = keyWord;
    const event = new Event("input", { bubbles: true });
    document.getElementById("search-input").dispatchEvent(event);
    // 搜索按钮DOM - 点击
    document.querySelectorAll(".search-icon")[0].click();
  };
  // 1.生成动态关键词输入UI-------------------------
  // (1.1). 容器
  const keyWordDom = document.createElement("div");
  const keyWordDomStyle = `
          width: 0; height: 0; opacity: 0; overflow: hidden;
          background-color: #f0c9cf; border-radius: 10px;
          position: fixed; right: 50vw; top: 50vh;
          box-shadow: 2px 6px 10px 0px #0e121629;
          transform: translate(50%, -50%); transition: all 0.3s;
      `;
  keyWordDom.style = keyWordDomStyle;
  // (1.2). 标题
  const keyWordTitleDom = document.createElement("div");
  keyWordTitleDom.style = `
          font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; padding: 10px;
        `;
  keyWordTitleDom.innerText = "小红书脚本检索关键词自定义(分号隔开;)";
  // (1.3). 输入文本域
  const keyWordInputArea = document.createElement("textarea");
  keyWordInputArea.style = `
          width: 580px; height: 300px; margin: 8px;
          resize:none; border: none;
        `;
  // (1.4). 状态申明
  const statusDom = document.createElement("div");
  statusDom.innerHTML = "<span style='color: #F56C6C'>当前运行状态: 已暂停(X)</span>";
  statusDom.style = `
          font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; padding-left: 10px;
        `;
  // (1.5). 启动按钮
  const keyWordStartBtn = document.createElement("div");
  keyWordStartBtn.style = `
          width: 60px; font-size: 16px; background-color: rgb(64,158,255);
          border-radius: 6px; padding: 4px; float: right; margin-right: 10px;
          cursor: pointer; text-align: center; color: white;
        `;
  keyWordStartBtn.innerText = "启动";
  keyWordStartBtn.onclick = async () => {
    if (document.querySelectorAll(".login-btn").length > 0) return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 请先登录");
    if (runStatus) return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 请先暂停脚本执行后,再进行启动操作");

    // 1.获取输入文本域内容
    const inputText = keyWordInputArea.value;
    const keyWordAry = inputText.split(";");
    let keyWordIndex = 0;
    if (keyWordAry[keyWordIndex] === "") return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 关键词不能存在空值");
    console.log(`%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]脚本已启动 => 关键词列表: `, "color: green", keyWordAry);
    runStatus = true;
    statusDom.innerHTML = "<span style='color: green'>当前运行状态: 执行中(√)</span>";
    handleSearch(keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]);
    await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
    // 2.将分类切换到最新
    const classDomList = document.querySelectorAll(".dropdown-items .text");
    for (let i = 0; i < classDomList.length; i++) {
      const dom = classDomList[i];
      const { textContent } = dom;
      if (textContent.includes("最新")) {
        dom.click();
        await sleep(3000); // 保证小红书接口请求最新数据后, 再执行后续逻辑
        break;
      }
    }
    // 3.进行点赞
    while (true) {
      // 如果状态为暂停, 则停止点赞行为
      if (!runStatus) break;
      // (3.1).获取点赞爱心DOM
      const likeDomList = document.querySelectorAll(".like-wrapper");
      // (3.2).如果点赞爱心DOM为0, 则相当于(3.5)
      if (likeDomList.length === 0) {
        console.warn("error: 未找到任何点赞按钮-页面DOM缺失,类名[.like-wrapper]");
        keyWordIndex++;
        if (keyWordIndex >= keyWordAry.length) {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]全部关键词已检索完毕,重新开始检索=>下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
          keyWordIndex = 0;
          await sleep(SEARCH_END_TIME);
        } else {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]当前关键词=>${
              keyWordAry[keyWordIndex - 1]
            }<=检索完毕, 切换到下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
        }
        handleSearch(keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]);
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
        continue;
      }
      // (3.3).将点赞爱心DOM排除掉已为点赞状态的DOM, 避免误操作取消点赞
      const waitLikeDomList = Array.from(likeDomList).filter((dom) => {
        const { baseVal } = dom.querySelectorAll("use")[0].href;
        return baseVal === "#like";
      });
      // (3.4).通知即将点赞数量, 执行点赞逻辑,以及通知本页已点赞数量
      console.log("本轮待点赞:", waitLikeDomList.length, "条数据");
      for (let i = 0; i < waitLikeDomList.length; i++) {
        const dom = waitLikeDomList[i];
        dom.click();
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
      }
      alreadyTotal += likeDomList.length;
      // (3.5).如果发现THE_END文案, 说明该分类的检索关键词数据已经全部获取完毕, 进行下一个关键字的检索
      if (document.querySelectorAll(".end-container").length > 0) {
        keyWordIndex++;
        if (keyWordIndex >= keyWordAry.length) {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]全部关键词已检索完毕,重新开始检索=>下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
          keyWordIndex = 0;
          await sleep(SEARCH_END_TIME);
        } else {
          console.log(
            `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]当前关键词=>${
              keyWordAry[keyWordIndex - 1]
            }<=检索完毕, 切换到下一个关键词 => `,
            "color: green",
            keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]
          );
        }
        handleSearch(keyWordAry[keyWordIndex]);
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
      }
      // (3.6).进行下一页的数据获取
      else {
        // 加载更多待点赞数据
        window.scrollBy(0, window.innerHeight);
        console.log(
          `%c[小红书脚本-${new Date().toLocaleString()}]已点赞数量: ${alreadyTotal}, 正在拉取下一页数据`,
          "color: tomato"
        );
        await sleep(SLEEP_TIME);
      }
    }
  };
  // (1.6). 停止按钮
  const keyWordStopBtn = document.createElement("div");
  keyWordStopBtn.style = `
          width: 60px; font-size: 16px; background-color: rgb(245,108,108);
          border-radius: 6px; padding: 4px; float: right; margin-right: 10px;
          cursor: pointer; text-align: center; color: white;
        `;
  keyWordStopBtn.innerText = "暂停";
  keyWordStopBtn.onclick = () => {
    if (!runStatus) return window.alert("小红书脚本提示: 当前已暂停运行");
    runStatus = false;
    statusDom.innerHTML = "<span style='color: #F56C6C'>当前运行状态: 已暂停(X)</span>";
  };

  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordTitleDom);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordInputArea);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordStartBtn);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(keyWordStopBtn);
  keyWordDom.appendChild(statusDom);
  // 2.生成入口UI-----------------------------------
  const entranceDom = document.createElement("div");
  const baseStyle = `
          position: fixed; right: 0; top: 40vh; cursor: pointer;
          width: 76px; background-color: rgb(212,25,27); white-space: nowrap;
          overflow: hidden; opacity: 0.4; transition: all 0.5s;
          padding: 4px 0px 4px 10px; border-radius: 10px 0px 0px 10px;
          font-size: 20px; font-weight: bold; color: white;
          box-shadow: 2px 6px 10px 0px #0e121629;
        `;
  entranceDom.style = baseStyle;
  entranceDom.title = "小红书自动点赞刷新脚本";
  entranceDom.innerText = "小红书 V2.0.0";
  entranceDom.onmouseover = () => {
    entranceDom.style = baseStyle + `opacity: 1; width: 160px;`;
  };
  entranceDom.onmouseleave = () => {
    entranceDom.style = baseStyle;
  };
  entranceDom.onclick = () => {
    openKeyWord = !openKeyWord;
    if (openKeyWord) {
      keyWordDom.style = keyWordDomStyle + "width: 600px; height: 410px; opacity: 0.8;";
    } else {
      keyWordDom.style = keyWordDomStyle + "width: 0; height: 0; opacity: 0;";
    }
  };
  // End: ========注入页面之中========
  document.body.appendChild(entranceDom);
  document.body.appendChild(keyWordDom);
})();
